  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2324258844" />
    <a title="Sharon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23218431-sharon"><img alt="Sharon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563502369p2/23218431.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2324258844?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon" href="/user/show/23218431-sharon">Sharon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=favorite-heroines">favorite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=happily-ever-after">happily-ever-after</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=multiple-romance">multiple-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=best-of-2018">best-of-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=family">family</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=tears-worthy">tears-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23218431-sharon?shelf=heartwarming">heartwarming</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2324258844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15111810134971711013">OK I am getting seriously addicted to this series, which is sad because there’s only 1 more book left after this!<br/><br/>Here are some of my thoughts:<br/>•	I LOVE the protagonist, Gillian. The book starts with the flashback, and I thought she was so annoying as a kid. However, she turns out to be so brave and caring of people. I love how she has saved Alec and has always put others before herself. She has shown over and over how badass she is. She’s not a physical fighter, but she is literally more courageo</span>
  <span id="freeText15111810134971711013" style="display:none">OK I am getting seriously addicted to this series, which is sad because there’s only 1 more book left after this!<br /><br />Here are some of my thoughts:<br />•	I LOVE the protagonist, Gillian. The book starts with the flashback, and I thought she was so annoying as a kid. However, she turns out to be so brave and caring of people. I love how she has saved Alec and has always put others before herself. She has shown over and over how badass she is. She’s not a physical fighter, but she is literally more courageous and noble than most warriors.<br />•	Alec. Agh. All of Gillian’s scenes with Alec is the cutest thing ever. I love how protective they are of each other. He is so adorable. I really wish we got to see more scenes with them after she has left his home. There really should have been more or a reunion later on because they meant so much to each other in the beginning.<br />•	Seeing Iain and Judith again is the best. Also, the reunion scene with them and Alec had me so emotional.<br />•	I’m so thankful that this is Brodick’s story. Based on the order of the scenes in the beginning, I thought this was a book about Gillian and Ramsey – which would so blah. THEN, I thought perhaps there was going to be a love triangle between Gillian, Ramsey, and Bridgid <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[who I honestly thought was going to be her sister. I think everyone thought that, so applause for Garwood for misleading us here. Great plot twist for when we did meet the sister <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. THANKFULLY, it’s Gillian and Brodick. I love Brodick from the first book because he’s so grumpy and sweet at the same time. And Gillian – I obviously love from what I already said. So together, they are just perfect. I like that she feels safe with him and his grumpiness and scary exterior don’t faze her. And I like that he recognizes how strong she is after seeing how hard she has worked to protect Alec.<br />•	Ramsey and Bridgid, on the other hand, are… boring. It just comes off cliché and besides the physical beauty of both of them, and their obvious interest for one another – I don’t feel or see much here. <br />•	I love the Buchanan warriors. They’re all so tough, but honestly sweet and hilarious. Their interactions with Gillian has been interesting.<br />•	I ADOOOORE Uncle Morgan. He is another cute grumpy, sweet man.<br />•	 I have to admit the last 25% besides the very ending has been not as good as the 1st 75%. I was literally at the edge of my seat for the 1st 75%.<br />•	The scene with Father Laggan is HILARIOUS. He was so wary and disbelieving that anyone would willingly want to get tied with a Buchanan. And then, his reaction when he realized he got duped was just… the best.<br /><br />Overall, I’m giving this <b>4 stars</b>. I honestly enjoyed it, and I love the characterization of Gillian and Brodick.<br /><br /><u>Things that you might want to know <b>(WARNING: Spoilers below)</b></u><br />Happy/satisfying ending? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No extended extending, so I would have liked more, but the ending is happy and cute. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Love triangle? Cheating? Angst level? Other things to note?<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, no, medium.<br /><br />There was only mention of a girl Brodick almost married but he said he wasn’t very into her and when she screwed up, his pride was hurt but he wasn’t missing her.<br /><br />For Ramsey, he almost had sex with this one woman, but Bridgid scared her off thinking Ramsey didn’t want the woman (but he did). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Tears-worthy? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Did get emotional at times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Humor? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes, some humorous moments. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Favorite scenes? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The Father Laggan scene when he was shocked and hysterical finding out that Brodick tricked him and Gillian in the marriage. When Gillian first meets Brodick at the church, and she later tells everyone the story about what she did for Alec. When Gillian bravely escaped with Alec. All the cute Alec and Gillian’s scenes as she’s protecting him. The reunion scene with Alec and his parents and his parents were SHOCKED and so happy and emotional to find out he’s alive. The party after where they celebrated, and everyone got to know Gillian. The very ending with Brodick finally admitting his feelings. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />What age level would be appropriate? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mature audience. Explicit details on sex. Vague mentions of rape (no actual scenes). Murders, plotting. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="15111810134971711013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3210405483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15588599525071342580">GAH! This book!It was published over 20 years ago but it's a romance that will forever stand the test of time! Brodick was my very sexy, very manly, very alpha male Highlander. He was Laird of a clan whose soldiers were compared to the Spartans. Ruthless savages who were able to defeat armies ten times their size. Yet this giant of a man who stood a head taller than other men became so tender and vulnerable for a woman who stole his heart.<br/><br/>There is so much humor in this book! The Highlanders desp</span>
  <span id="freeText15588599525071342580" style="display:none">GAH! This book!It was published over 20 years ago but it's a romance that will forever stand the test of time! Brodick was my very sexy, very manly, very alpha male Highlander. He was Laird of a clan whose soldiers were compared to the Spartans. Ruthless savages who were able to defeat armies ten times their size. Yet this giant of a man who stood a head taller than other men became so tender and vulnerable for a woman who stole his heart.<br /><br />There is so much humor in this book! The Highlanders despise England and all the stories bashing the English make for some very amusing moments. The fact that this Highlander chose an English bride was just downright hilarious!<br /><br />There is SWOON-WORTHY romance with suspense, action and adventure! A heroine that is so fierce, intelligent and braver than any man! I can't recommend this book enough. Books like this are why I love historical romance!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15588599525071342580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_436572637" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436572637" />
    <a title="Susanne " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7179798-susanne"><img alt="Susanne " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511902036p2/7179798.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436572637?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susanne " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susanne " href="/user/show/7179798-susanne">Susanne </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Susanne  by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4651519-tiko">Tiko</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7179798-susanne?shelf=genre-historical-romance">genre-historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436572637" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7322439976217130802"><i>Highlander romance. 5 stars</i><br/><br/>Wow! This book is long but it never felt dragged out. It's about Lady Gillian whose father was killed when their home was invaded when she was just a little girl. His father gives her big sister Christen a treasure but the two sisters are separated in the flight and Gillian is captured. When we meet her again she's grown up and held captive by the baron who killed her father. He's taken her uncle hostage and if she doesn't bring back her sister and the treasure he will</span>
  <span id="freeText7322439976217130802" style="display:none"><i>Highlander romance. 5 stars</i><br /><br />Wow! This book is long but it never felt dragged out. It's about Lady Gillian whose father was killed when their home was invaded when she was just a little girl. His father gives her big sister Christen a treasure but the two sisters are separated in the flight and Gillian is captured. When we meet her again she's grown up and held captive by the baron who killed her father. He's taken her uncle hostage and if she doesn't bring back her sister and the treasure he will kill him.<br /><br />But this is a highland romance? Yes, Christen is hiding in the Scottish highlands. <b> Yes, we will meet Iain and Judith from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/107770.The_Secret__Highlands__Lairds__1_" title="The Secret (Highlands' Lairds #1) by Julie Garwood" rel="nofollow noopener">The Secret</a> and we will spend a lot of time with hunky warriors Brodick and Ramsey.</b> There is a second romance as well and a very tight mystery plot.<br /><br />I really loved the first part of this book and I was sure it was going to knock down <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/107779.The_Bride__Lairds__Fianc_es___1_" title="The Bride (Lairds' Fiancées, #1) by Julie Garwood" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bride</a> as my favorite JG romance. But it didn't. I mean it was awesome but there was a little thing that bothered me and that was (minor) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that Gillian was too stubborn and reckless. In the end I was almost ready to strangle her. I mean she has the three strongest lairds and their armies at her hand but no she doesn't trust them and has to sacrifice herself on a stupid plan <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I get that it was medieval times but I would have liked for Brodick and Gillian to actually talk to each other, not only boss each other around. And where was the epilogue?</span>
  <a data-text-id="7322439976217130802" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vT/MQgbRH33Y+Jf6l36GeLk0JsunV3Ng2jV/IQ+T6hllY3NsBZlSdT3QxOcGG6jPSDOWiIADUI5OHpcx7VmdrQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('txTfKdV62XcflQGnXTGed+5pVqQ6jbGEMXxyafhH+aZvSGAH1jKUf/q9UrrMVLDAH27m5x3ZkmqlV5p5Go2OEg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Sheridan was knocked unconscious on the quayside, and recovered to find herself in the handsome stranger\'s care, not knowing who she was.\n\nIt was to be the beginning of a dazzling, witty, dramatic, <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14885120182729536249">With more than 35 million books in print and 26 NEW YORK TIMES bestsellers, Julie Garwood has earned a position among America's favorite fiction writers.<br/><br/>Born and raised in Kansas City, MO, Ms. Garwood attributes much of her success to growing up in a large family of Irish heritage. "The Irish are great storytellers who relish getting all of the details and nuances of every situation. Add in the fa</span>
  <span id="freeText14885120182729536249" style="display:none">With more than 35 million books in print and 26 NEW YORK TIMES bestsellers, Julie Garwood has earned a position among America's favorite fiction writers.<br /><br />Born and raised in Kansas City, MO, Ms. Garwood attributes much of her success to growing up in a large family of Irish heritage. "The Irish are great storytellers who relish getting all of the details and nuances of every situation. Add in the fact that I was the sixth of seven children. Early in life, I learned that self expression had to be forceful, imaginative, and quick," says Ms. Garwood. <br /><br />She began her writing career when the youngest of her three children entered school. After the publications of two young-adult books, she turned her talents to historical fiction. Her first novel, GENTLE WARRIOR, was published by Pocket Books in 1985. Since then, she has branched into other genres including contemporary romantic suspense. Today, her name appears regularly on the bestseller lists of every major publication in the country, and her books are translated into dozens of languages around the world. Her bestselling novel FOR THE ROSES was adapted for the HALLMARK HALL OF FAME television movie ROSE HILL.<br /><br />Ms. Garwood lives in Leawood, KS and is currently working on her next novel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14885120182729536249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
